PFx Brick on Kickstarter</a></h1><small>Posted by <a href=\"/profile/Huw\" rel=\"author\">Huw</a>, <time datetime=\"2017-04-20 08:05\">20 Apr 2017 08:05</time></small></header><a href=\"https://www.kickstarter.com/projects/fxbricks/pfx-brick\" title=\"Link to external website, opens in a new tab.\" rel=\"nofollow\"><img alt=\"\" src=\"https://images.brickset.com/news/33554852211-pfx-brick-kickstarter-campaign.jpg\" class=\"mainimg\"></a><footer><div class=\"tags\"><a class=\"meta\">2582 Views</div></footer>\n<p><a href=\"https://brickset.com/article/27274/pfx-brick-on-kickstarter\">Last month we told you about </a>an exciting programmable brick, <a href=\"https://www.kickstarter.com/projects/fxbricks/pfx-brick\" title=\"Link to external website, opens in a new tab.\" rel=\"nofollow\">PFx Brick</a>, on Kickstarter that's been designed by well respected members of the AFOL community Jason Allemann (of Ideas Maze fame) and Michael Gale.</p>\n<p>PFx Brick is a programmable electronic brick controller designed to offer three major functions for LEGO models: motor control, lighting effects and sound effects.</p>\n<p>Funding for the project ends in six days and it's achieved 38% of the required total of CA$140K so far, so if you're interested in seeing it to production and getting hold of one then now would be a good time to pledge your support.</p>\n<p>Since we mentioned it last time, Bluetooth support has been added which now makes it much more versatile.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.kickstarter.com/projects/fxbricks/pfx-brick\" title=\"Link to external website, opens in a new tab.\" rel=\"nofollow\">Head on over to Kickstarter</a> to do so, and to find out more about the brick's capabilities.</p>\n<div class=\"links\">\n<p><a href=\"/article/27624/reminder-pfx-brick-on-kickstarter#comments\">12 comments</a>,
